{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2021-04-13 00:43:06","updatedTime":"2021-04-13 00:43:06","title":"The ultimate guide to Amazon's advertising business, which is $21 billion and growing","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/inside-amazons-growing-ad-business-everything-we-know-2019-5","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5dc597be7eece507a8661956?format=jpeg\" alt=\"amazon advertising executive 2x1\" height=\"600\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Alex Wong/Getty Images; Samantha Lee/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><section><section><p>Amazon&#39;s e-commerce dominance is quickly expanding to advertising.</p><p>The pandemic has drastically cut ad budgets as marketers reign back their spending, but e-commerce advertising is booming as people shop more from home - with Amazon leading the pack.</p><p>EMarketer said Amazon claimed 10.3% of the US digital ad market in 2020, up from 7.8% in 2019 - competing with Google and Facebook for ad budgets. That growth has attracted Walmart, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/top-instacart-advertising-execs-to-know-2021-3\">Instacart, </a>Walgreens and other retailers that have joined Amazon in vying for a slice of the pie.</p><p>Here&#39;s the latest on what we know about Amazon&#39;s moves to grow its advertising business.</p><h2>How big is advertising for Amazon?</h2><p>Amazon made about $21.5 billion from advertising in 2020, up from roughly $9.3 billion in the year-ago period.</p><p>While that amount is a tiny sliver of Amazon&#39;s revenue from retail sales and Amazon Web Services, its cloud business, advertising is one of its fastest-growing areas. The tech giant continues to cut into advertisers&#39; search budgets that mostly go to Google.</p><ul><li><em><strong>Read more: </strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-hire-an-amazon-advertising-agency-2021-1\">The complete guide to hiring an Amazon agency</a></em></li><li><em> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazons-ad-dominance-growing-2019-cowen-ad-buyer-survey-2020-1\">7 charts show why Amazon&#39;s ad business could balloon to $17 billion this year and is a growing threat to Google</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/inside-amazons-charm-offensive-to-win-over-madison-avenue-2019-4?r=amazon-ad-library\">Inside Amazon&#39;s charm offensive to win over big brand budgets from Madison Avenue</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/why-amazon-creates-groups-of-advertising-teams-2019-4?r=amazon-ad-library\">Marketers say Amazon&#39;s advertising business is difficult to navigate. Here&#39;s why the company thinks the &#39;chaotic&#39; structure actually makes sense.</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-trying-to-win-over-small-advertisers-cowen-2019-2019-8\">A Wall Street firm says Amazon is stepping up its efforts to win small advertisers with cheaper prices and help from sales reps</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-increases-google-shopping-ads-for-prime-day-2019-merkle-2019-7\">Amazon is pumping money into Google to promote Prime Day, and it could be a brilliant way to also boost Amazon&#39;s own ad business</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazons-ad-business-will-quadruple-by-2023-brian-wieser-pivotal-research-2019-1?r=amazon-ad-library\">Amazon&#39;s ad business is set to more than quadruple by 2023 - and Google should be worried</a></em></li></ul><h2>The pandemic&#39;s impact on Amazon</h2><p>While advertisers have slashed TV and some digital budgets during the pandemic, Amazon&#39;s advertising has grown as people do more of their shopping online. Amazon has also increased the advertising potential of Twitch, its live-streaming service whose viewership has grown during the pandemic.</p><ul><li><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazons-2020-advertising-spend-rebounds-after-coronavirus-hit-2020-8\">Amazon has been on an advertising blitz, and it&#39;s benefitting platforms like Instagram</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/ad-buyers-explain-amazons-ad-business-impact-from-coronavirus-2020-5\">Amazon&#39;s ad business is spiking, but ad buyers say the coronavirus reveals the commerce giant&#39;s weaknesses versus Google and Facebook</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazons-2020-pitch-deck-twitch-has-159-million-monthly-users-2020-9\">Leaked pitch deck slides from Amazon&#39;s Twitch reveal new data about the live-streaming site&#39;s audience</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/coronavirus-2020-amazon-agency-gives-advice-to-third-party-sellers-2020-3\">An Amazon-focused agency shares tips for sellers facing turbulent sales under coronavirus</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/coronavirus-2020-amazon-sellers-talk-about-unexpected-sales-2020-3\">&#39;It&#39;s a total bloodbath:&#39; 5 Amazon sellers and experts share stories of turbulent sales amid the coronavirus outbreak</a></em></li></ul><h2>Ad tech&#39;s role in Amazon&#39;s ad business</h2><p>Advertisers and sellers often cite a lack of data and tools as challenges in advertising on Amazon, which has given rise to a cottage industry of firms that specialize in helping marketers navigate the site. Meanwhile, Amazon has pushed further into programmatic advertising with its OTT arm that sells ads in some Fire TV apps.</p><ul><li><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/18-companies-powering-amazons-2020-advertising-and-seller-business-2020-5\">Meet 18 firms solving companies&#39; giant problems selling and advertising on Amazon</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-focused-startups-like-teikametrics-and-etailz-raise-money-2020-2\">Amazon is breeding a new crop of marketing startups, and investors are buying in</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-is-pitching-advertisers-more-on-alexa-audio-ads-2020-2\">Amazon is ramping up its pitch for audio ads after long promising Alexa would be ad-free</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazons-ott-pitch-deck-pushes-branded-alexa-skills-2020-1\">Amazon&#39;s new OTT pitch deck shows how the e-commerce giant is letting advertisers use Alexa to market their products</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazons-2019-ott-pitch-deck-2019-5?r=amazon-ad-library\">Amazon wants to take on OTT heavyweights like Roku for advertising dollars. Still, advertisers say that Amazon&#39;s data can be limited and continue to find new ways to measure ads.</p><ul><li><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-rolls-out-roas-metric-on-advertising-service-2020-8\">Amazon started showing a favored metric for advertisers this month, making it easier for large brands to compare ad efficiency against Google and Facebook</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazons-attribution-tool-tracks-sales-from-facebook-and-google-ads-2019-9\">Amazon is rolling out a tool that shows just how much Google and Facebook ads drive people to do their shopping on the e-commerce site</a></em></li><li><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-is-letting-brands-track-facebook-traffic-2019-3?r=amazon-ad-library\">Amazon is finally letting brands track traffic from Facebook in its latest effort to cozy up to big marketers</a></em></li></ul><h2>Who runs Amazon&#39;s ad business?</h2><p>Amazon is notoriously secretive as a workplace. As Amazon&#39;s advertising ambitions have grown, it&#39;s cultivated a team of execs who pitch advertisers on its ad business.</p><p>They include several longtime Amazon employees, including Colleen Aubrey, who is part of Amazon&#39;s executive suite. buying brand new. </p><p>Refurbished items are generally returns, faulty open-box products, or brand new units with minor cosmetic flaws that have been returned to &#34;like new&#34; quality by the manufacturer. We&#39;re a fan of them here at Insider Reviews - we&#39;ve even written reviews of our personal refurb purchases from <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/apple-best-discounts-refurbished-ios-mac-devices\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Apple</a> and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/nintendo-switch-refurbished-is-a-great-little-deal-2018-10\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Nintendo</a>.</p><p>Buying refurbished has its benefits. For most shoppers, the most convincing benefit is the lower cost. Depending on the item and the manufacturer, a refurbished item can cost you up to 50% less than a brand new one. Another perk is that it&#39;s a bit more environmentally friendly: you&#39;re essentially buying a recycled item.  In the end, both refurbished and new items will ideally deliver the same user experience, likely with some differences in packaging and cosmetics, so long as you do your research before adding to cart.</p><p>When determining a refurb&#39;s worthiness, it comes down to two major factors to make the judgment call: who refurbished the item and who is selling it?</p><bi-shortcode id=\"table-of-contents-sticky\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-type=\"h2\">Table of Contents: Masthead Sticky</bi-shortcode>\n<div id=\"slideshow\">\n\tThe best refurb deals available right now\n\t\n\t<p>When shopping refurb deals, we keep an eye out for items that are discounted compared to typical refurb pricing, which is generally much less than brand new. data-purchase-option=\"Best Buy\">AirPods Pro (Refurbished) (medium, Preferred: Best Buy)</bi-shortcode>\n\tWho should I trust to refurbish an item?\n\t\n\t<p>When it comes to buying an item refurbished, there is no source more reliable than the manufacturer. Year-round, manufacturers like Dyson, Nintendo, and Apple offer refurbished goods for considerably less money than in new condition. I, personally, bought a refurbished Dyson V6 cordless stick vacuum 3 years ago during Black Friday, and not only did the item arrive looking new, but it also still performs well despite daily use.&#160;</p><p>Manufacturer refurbs can also come with pretty hefty warranties. <a href=\"https://click.linksynergy.com/deeplink?id=EHFxW6yx8Uo&#38;mid=36310&#38;murl=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.dyson.com%2Fdyson-outlet%23shop-all-refurbished\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Dyson</a>, for example, provides a 6- or 12-month warranty with every order, along with expert support and the promise of genuine Dyson parts in your item.</p><p>If you're a frequent online shopper, you've surely come across a few items marked as \"seller-refurbished.\" Our advice: outside of a few exceptions, don't risk it. While you don't necessarily need to limit yourself to only buying from manufacturer storefronts, buying an item refurbished by anyone other than the manufacturer is dubious. Certain special cases like <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1724133199543959581\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Geek Squad Certified Refurbished</a> and <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/b/ref=s9_acss_bw_cg_arhome_2a1_w?node=17871142011&#38;pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&#38;pf_rd_s=merchandised-search-6&#38;pf_rd_r=VCA416Y6JK0THK5JJ3XZ&#38;pf_rd_t=101&#38;pf_rd_p=ac369fbe-1701-43cd-b884-9b142d8b86d2&#38;pf_rd_i=12653393011&#38;_encoding=UTF8&#38;tag=biip_111820_why-refurbished-items-are-worth-buying-20&#38;linkCode=ur2&#38;linkId=64b468e3e152ea594fcac737fd845763&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon Renewed</a> are worth considering, but these have less specialized support and notably shorter warranty coverage (typically, only 90 days).&#160;</p>\n\tWhere can I buy refurbs from?\n\t\n\t<p>The easiest, most reliable places to find refurbished items for sale are from the manufacturer's storefronts. Vacuums (both cordless and upright), fans, heaters, stand mixers, blenders, and the like are pretty dependable refurbished, and they arrive in like-new condition.</p><p>Laptops, computers, smartphones, tablets, gaming consoles, and accessories are typical to find refurbished, and they're often worth considering. The warranties never last as long, it doesn't guarantee the use of genuine parts, and the product support you receive will never be as good &#8212; if you get any at all.&#160;</p><p>Much older generation tech is also not worth buying refurbished. It's 2020: buying a refurbished iPhone 7 is a moot investment in an item nearing obsoletion.</p><p>Finally, don't bother with anything that can't have its battery replaced, like truly wireless earbuds and headphones. It's a mixed bag getting these in any condition other than new; you'll never know the battery's remaining lifespan. REUTERS/Lucas Jackson\" height=\"542\" width=\"722\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Microsoft will buy Nuance Communications for $19.7 billion.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomson Reuters</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Microsoft has agreed to buy Nuance Communications for $19.7 billion.</li>\n<li>Microsoft intends to integrate Nuance&#39;s technology into its healthcare-specific cloud strategy.</li>\n<li>The acquisition is Microsoft&#39;s second-largest after the $24 billion purchase of LinkedIn.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Microsoft has agreed to buy the AI and voice communications firm Nuance for $19.7 billion.</p><p>The deal, expected to close at the end of the year, would value Nuance at $56 per share, implying a premium of 23% to the stock&#39;s closing price on April 9.</p><p>Nuance is Microsoft&#39;s second largest acquisition after its <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/microsoft-buys-linkedin-2016-6\">$24 billion purchase</a> of LinkedIn in 2016.</p><p>Nuance&#39;s speech recognition engine is the basis for Apple&#39;s voice assistant Siri, and the company has developed Dragon Naturally Speaking voice technology products.</p><p>Microsoft intends to integrate Nuance&#39;s technology into its healthcare-specific cloud strategy. More than half of physicians and 77% of US hospitals use Nuance&#39;s technology, according to a <a href=\"https://news.microsoft.com/2021/04/12/microsoft-accelerates-industry-cloud-strategy-for-healthcare-with-the-acquisition-of-nuance/\">release</a>. Revenue for Nuance&#39;s Healthcare Cloud grew 37% year-over-year at the end of 2020.</p><p>&#34;Nuance provides the AI layer at the healthcare point of delivery and is a pioneer in the real-world application of enterprise AI,&#34; Microsoft CEO Satya Nadella said in a statement. &#34;Together, with our partner ecosystem, we will put advanced AI solutions into the hands of professionals everywhere to drive better decision-making and create more meaningful connections, as we accelerate growth of Microsoft Cloud in Healthcare and Nuance.&#34;</p><p>Nadella told CNBC he expects the pandemic to accelerate the &#34;digital transformation&#34; of healthcare, and improving health outcomes will require help from tech companies.</p><p>&#34;Not only will we be able to serve all the providers with everything we do in Microsoft 365 dynamics, 365 Azure, but Nuance will be able to help us deliver these AI-first solutions for doctors and radiologists and overall clinical decision support in partnership with the rest of the ecosystem,&#34; Nadella said.</p><p>Nuance CEO Mark Benjamin, who will remain at the helm after the deal with Microsoft closes, said the partnership will allow the firm to hyper-scale existing technology on a global scale and provide better access to care.</p><p>Benjamin added he hopes to decrease burnout among physicians by reducing the amount of charting, which tends to add two hours of work per one hour of patient care.</p><p>&#34;We believe that our solutions coupled with Microsoft&#39;s platform and capabilities will bring actually the It's also about as low-maintenance as it gets when it comes to application; the rollerball applicator glides right onto the skin and the formula is easily blendable with just your fingertips. Plus, its light, citrus scent makes for an all-around pleasant experience.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"small\" data-pid=\"605ca624065f5700185197bd\" data-purchase-option=\"\">Sunshine Skin Tint Clean SPF 30 Foundation (small)</bi-shortcode>\n\tILIA Super Serum Skin Tint\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606497dfdaf0f10018f993ae?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Best tinted moisturizer_Llia\" height=\"1251\" width=\"1668\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">ILIA; Catherine Santino/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>Most tinted moisturizers boast skincare benefits, but <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1735902063025354283\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">ILIA's Skin Tint</a> takes things to the next level.&#160;</h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li><strong>SPF: </strong>40</li><li><strong>Color range: </strong>30 shades, from Skye, a very fair neutral shade, to Lovina, a deep shade with neutral undertones.&#160;</li></ul></aside><p>This tinted moisturizer is worth every penny. Not only does it offer a stunning lit-from-within glow, but <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1735902063025354283\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">ILIA's Super Serum Skin Tint</a> is also boosted with skin-nourishing superheroes Hyaluronic Acid, plant-based squalane, and niacinamide. The downsides? A somewhat messy dropper applicator and a strong SPF scent. Even still, this product stands tall above the rest.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"small\" data-pid=\"605ca7753d35010018fe0b52\" data-purchase-option=\"\">Super Serum Skin Tint (small)</bi-shortcode>\n\tFirst Aid Beauty Ultra Repair Tinted Moisturizer SPF 30\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60649807daf0f10018f993b0?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Best tinted moisturizer_FirstAidBeauty\" height=\"1251\" width=\"1667\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">First Aid Beauty; Catherine Santino/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>Sensitive skin? Look no further than <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1735909531405098895\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">First Aid Beauty Ultra Repair Tinted Moisturizer</a>.&#160;</h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li><strong>SPF: </strong>30</li><li><strong>Color range: </strong>10 shades, from ivory to deep.&#160;</li></ul></aside><p>First Aid Beauty puts the \"moisturizer\" in tinted moisturizer. Known for being sensitive-skin friendly, the brand certainly does not disappoint with this member of the Ultra Repair line. The light, airy texture is so similar to that of a face cream that you might just forget you're wearing makeup &#8212; which is probably the entire point.&#160;</p><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"small\" data-pid=\"605ca9460067080018af048a\" data-purchase-option=\"\">Ultra Repair Tinted Moisturizer SPF 30 (small)</bi-shortcode>\n\tBareMinerals Complexion Rescue Tinted Hydrating Gel Cream\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6064981fdaf0f10018f993b1?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Best tinted moisturizer_BareMinerals\" height=\"1250\" width=\"1667\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">BareMinerals; Catherine Santino/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1735909607231173521\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">BareMinerals Complexion Rescue Tinted Hydrating Gel Cream</a> is the epitome of light, dewy coverage.</h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li><strong>SPF: </strong>40</li><li><strong>Color range: </strong>20 shades, from Opal, a fair shade with pink undertones, to Mahogany, a very deep hue with peachy undertones.&#160;</li></ul></aside><p>The perfect balance of hydration and natural coverage, this will surely become your daily go-to. It's great to throw on when you need to look put together quickly (i.e. last-minute Zoom meetings), but it's also easily buildable for a more full-coverage (but always dewy) complexion.&#160;</p><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"small\" data-pid=\"605cabfd3d35010018fe0b5b\" data-purchase-option=\"\">Complexion Rescue Tinted Hydrating Gel Cream (small)</bi-shortcode>\n\tChanel Les Beiges Sheer Healthy Glow Moisturizing Tint\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606498656183e10019819830?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Best tinted moisturizer_Chanel\" height=\"1250\" width=\"1667\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Chanel; Catherine Santino/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>Though it contains fragrance, you simply cannot beat the healthy glow of <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.nordstrom.com%2Fs%2Fchanel-les-beiges-sheer-healthy-glow-moisturizing-tint-broad-spectrum-spf-30%2F4926589\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Chanel's Les Beiges Sheer Healthy Glow Moisturizing Tint</a>.</h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li><strong>SPF: </strong>30</li><li><strong>Color range: </strong>6 shades, from light to deep</li></ul></aside><p>This product is worthy of accolades simply because it is precisely what it claims to be: a sheer, healthy glow. One swipe of the Chanel Les Beiges tinted moisturizer and your skin looks revitalized, luminous, and impossibly supple. There's not much coverage, and the shade range is very narrow compared to the other tinted moisturizers on this list, but the gorgeous finish is exactly what we wish for on natural makeup days.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"small\" data-pid=\"605cb1e73d35010018fe0b62\" data-purchase-option=\"\">Les Beiges Sheer Healthy Glow Moisturizing Tint (small)</bi-shortcode>\n\tKosas Tinted Face Oil\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6064987b6183e10019819832?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Best tinted moisturizer_Kosas\" height=\"1251\" width=\"1667\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Kosas; Catherine Santino/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1735905492519834457\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Kosas' Tinted Face Oil</a> is perhaps the most comfortable tinted moisturizer out there.</h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li><strong>SPF: </strong>None</li><li><strong>Color range: </strong>16 shades, from Tone 1, a porcelain with cool undertones, to Tone 10, an ultra-deep hue.&#160;</li></ul></aside><p>Kosas says their <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1735905492519834457\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Tinted Face Oil</a> is \"the sweatpants of foundation\", and there is truly no better description. The lightweight formula absorbs immediately into the skin and leaves behind a soft, silky texture &#8212; perfect for those who can't stand the feeling of foundation on their face. The name \"tinted face oil\" is also incredibly accurate, as what this product lacks in coverage it makes up for in glow.&#160;</p><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"small\" data-pid=\"605cb6430067080018af04a5\" data-purchase-option=\"\">Tinted Face Oil (small)</bi-shortcode>\n\tGlossier Perfecting Skin Tint\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6064988bdaf0f10018f993b4?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Best tinted moisturizer_Glossier\" height=\"1251\" width=\"1668\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Glossier; Catherine Santino/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.glossier.com%2Fproducts%2Fperfecting-skin-tint\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Glossier's Perfecting Skin Tint</a> is like your skin ... but better.<strong>&#160;</strong></h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li><strong>SPF: </strong>None</li><li><strong>Color range: </strong>12 shades, from G1, a rich, deep neutral, to G12, an ultra-fiar hue.&#160;</li></ul></aside><p>Similar to the Kosas Tinted Face Oil, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.glossier.com%2Fproducts%2Fperfecting-skin-tint\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Glossier's Perfecting Skin Tint</a> gives your skin a subtle, glowy boost &#8212; with even less coverage. Hopefully Clinique will start offering a wider shade range.&#160;</p><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"small\" data-pid=\"605cb98e065f5700185197ef\" data-purchase-option=\"\">Moisture Surge CC Cream Hydrating Color Corrector (small)</bi-shortcode>\n\tOther tinted moisturizers we considered\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6074483a3e3fe7001882a131?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Best tinted moisturizer_Other tinted moisturizers we considered\" height=\"834\" width=\"1668\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>From left to right: ITCosmetics Your Skin but Better CC Cream, Sephora Collection Weekend Warrior Tone Up Cream, and Tarte Amazonian Clay BB Tinted Moisturizer\n<p class=\"copyright\">Catherine Santino/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>The 10 tinted moisturizers above were my top picks, but I also tested 3 others. 00:43:06","updatedTime":"2021-04-13 00:43:06","title":"5 ways to make your marketing and branding more memorable","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/marketing-branding-small-business-more-memorable-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f86298f91aa9e001880b7c4?format=jpeg\" alt=\"marketing and advertising\" height=\"531\" width=\"709\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Marketing should be exploratory and dynamic to capture the interest of the new generation of customers.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Carlina Teteris</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Modern customers respond better to marketing that&#39;s more personalized and interactive.</li>\n<li>Customers tend to advocate for brands they have great relationships with via positive experiences. </li>\n<li>This type of marketing helps businesses build loyal and recurring customers.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>As a business consultant, I often have to remind small-business owners that their marketing needs to be more interactive, versus the traditional &#34;<a href=\"https://www.inc.com/michael-fertik/welcome-to-the-pull-economy.html\">push</a>&#34; model, where you broadcast your message to as many people as possible.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.inc.com/shama-hyder/how-to-market-to-gen-z.html\">New generations</a> of customers respond better to the &#34;<a href=\"https://www.inc.com/robert-glazer/these-3-new-marketing-trends-will-transform-your-marketing-strategy.html\">participative</a>&#34; approach, where they get to provide input via social media and the internet.</p><p>It started a few years ago with email satisfaction surveys after an online purchase, but now includes interactive internet ads, as well as custom requests for input on the design of future products and influencers on social media. It seems that everyone these days wants an experience and a relationship, and is willing to become your best advocate via word of mouth.</p><p>Some call it a move from always &#34;<a href=\"https://www.inc.com/jeff-pruitt/why-your-businesss-growth-potential-isnt-in-net-new.html\">hunting</a>&#34; for new customers in the wild to &#34;gardening,&#34; or nurturing loyalty and value from the ones you already have.</p><p>In any case, the new approach is important to all businesses, and embodies some new marketing rules that you need to focus on and learn:</p><h2>1. Make your marketing exploratory and dynamic</h2><p>The days of big-bang long-term campaigns that never change are over. You should be constantly trying new approaches via social media and online, and asking for feedback and input from influencers and customers. Scale quickly on good feedback, and move on if you get little engagement.</p><p>A step in the right direction is to take advantage of the new tools available at very low cost, including sponsored podcasts, blogs, visibility in online communities, and Twitter influencer support. Sometimes it&#39;s as simple as updating your website format and videos.</p><h2>2. Use experiments versus designing the ideal ad</h2><p>Trends and customer interests change quickly, so use small experiments to find something that works today, and use innovation to push the envelope, before your competitors can copy and overrun you. The key is to be able to measure your return, adapt quickly, and learn from your efforts.</p><p>According to the <a href=\"https://hbr.org/2020/10/marketers-underuse-ad-experiments-thats-a-big-mistake\">Harvard Business Review</a>, e-commerce companies that conducted ad experiments saw 2-3% better performance per experiment run. An advertiser that ran 15 experiments in a given year saw a 30% higher ad performance.</p><h2>3. Motivate customers to participate and engage</h2><p>Reward customers for their advocacy and engagement with discounts and coupons, keep the interaction dynamic, and encourage their return. This requires a sense of urgency on the part of your team, and a culture of accountability and focus on the customer. Marketing must be everyone&#39;s top priority.</p><p>For example, <a href=\"https://www.inc.com/robert-glazer/these-3-new-marketing-trends-will-transform-your-marketing-strategy.html\">Dunkin&#39; Donuts</a> did this through a photo contest, rewarding discounts to those who submitted a photo with the brand&#39;s handle and hashtag. Other companies highlight live experience and happy videos, submitted by customers, on their website and promotions.</p><h2>4. Partner with others to create blended offerings</h2><p>A very successful marketing effort created by a restaurant near me during the pandemic offered a carryout from multiple sources - to combine flowers with food and drinks, all from different establishments, packaged creatively together. Everybody wins, and it spread quickly on social media.</p><p>People remember and endorse you as the primary brand that created the blended offering, as well as the other &#34;endorsed&#34; brands. The hybrid approach is also effective as an experiment if you are exploring ways to expand your own brand into new segments.</p><h2>5. Market solutions as an experience or an event</h2><p>Advertising more features, or even a lower price, is not as memorable to customers today as a great experience or a unique event. These may be live or immersive online experiences. Use social media to build anticipation and highlight successes, to get people talking and coming back for more. <br> <br>The message here is that big blockbuster campaigns and big marketing budgets are no longer the key to results in the new customer environment, where participation and relationships are key.</p><p>Now is the time to ask your customers and partners for participative ideas, do some experiments, and scale up the ones that work. Be prepared to make frequent updates as trends change.</p><p>Marketing is no longer a one-way conversation, whether you are a startup or a legacy business. How long has it been since you changed your marketing strategy? Are your costs going up and the returns going down?<br>Try listening and learning, more than talking and pushing.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/msft-stock\">Microsoft</a> will purchase the AI speech-recognition software maker for $19.7 billion in cash, with the price to include Nuance&#39;s net debt.</p><p>Microsoft, in a joint statement, said it will buy Nuance for $56 a share, which is a 23% premium to Nuance&#39;s closing price on Friday at $45.58. <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2021-04-12/microsoft-makes-big-bet-on-health-care-ai-technology-with-nuance?sref=GUP2BhaG\">Bloomberg reported</a> late Sunday that the two companies were in talks, citing sources who asked not to be identified. An agreement with Nuance would be Microsoft&#39;s largest since it purchased professional networking site LinkedIn in 2016.</p><p>Nuance climbed 18% to $53.93 as regular-session trading got underway. The stock during pre-market trade climbed by as much as 31%. Meanwhile, Microsoft shares edged up 0.1% to $255.97 as Wall Street&#39;s new trading week kicked off. </p><p>Nuance and Microsoft have been working together since 2019, focusing on Nuance&#39;s products that allow clinicians to capture patient discussions and integrate them into electronic health records. Microsoft said the deal will double its total addressable market in the healthcare provider space to nearly $500 billion.</p><p>&#34;AI is technology&#39;s most important priority, and healthcare is its most urgent application,&#34; said Microsoft CEO Satya Nadella in the statement.</p><p>The deal is expected to close by the end of the calendar year 2021 and has been unanimously approved by the boards of both Nuance and Microsoft. Nuance&#39;s CEO Mark Benjamin will remain in his role.</p><p>&#34;For Nadella &#38; Co., this is the right acquisition at the right time with Microsoft doubling down on its healthcare initiatives over the coming years,&#34; said Wedbush analyst Dan Ives in a Monday note in which he called the Nuance deal a &#34;strategic no brainer&#34; for Microsoft. rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Sony's WF-1000XM3</a> are better when it comes to sound quality and noise cancellation</p><p>Apple's AirPods Pro are our top pick because they offer the best experience with the least compromise.&#160;</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FApple-AirPods-Pro%2F520468661\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">AirPods Pro</a> address many of our complaints about Apple's original AirPods since they offer adjustable ear tips, active noise cancellation, better sound quality, and sweat and water resistance. That makes them a great choice whether you're looking for a reliable pair of wireless earbuds for working out or drowning out distractions.</p><p>The biggest benefit that the AirPods Pro offer over the standard AirPods are active noise cancellation. During my time using them, I've found that the AirPods Pro are able to successfully dull the sound of the treadmill humming during my run, the noisiness of the New York City subway, and chatty coworkers. They don't seal out sound as efficiently as the AirPods Max given the latter model's over-ear design, but they do a great job for earbuds.</p><p>In addition to bringing active noise cancellation and swappable ear tips for a more customized fit, the AirPods Pro also sound better than their cheaper siblings.&#160;</p><p>Unlike the regular AirPods, the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FApple-AirPods-Pro%2F520468661\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">AirPods Pro</a> have a custom Apple driver and high dynamic range amplifier, which results in sound that feels more boisterous and rich compared to the standard AirPods. They also support spatial audio, a surround sound effect that adjusts as you move your head. The standard AirPods don't have this feature.</p><p>While the AirPods Pro's active noise cancellation and wide selection of features make them the best choice for most people, especially since you can often <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/apple-airpods-deals\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">find them at a discount</a>, that doesn't mean they're perfect.&#160;</p><p>Anyone who isn't partial to Apple should strongly consider <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/sony-wf-1000xm3-wireless-headphones-review\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Sony's WF-1000XM3 </a>wireless earbuds, which offer better noise cancellation, sound, and battery life compared to the AirPods Pro.</p>\n\tThe best AirPods on a budget\n\t<figure>\n\t<img with the iPhone.</h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Fit and style:</strong> Earbuds, non-customizable&#160;</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Battery life:</strong> Up to 5 hours, more than 24 hours with charging case</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Water resistant:</strong> No</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Features:</strong> Hey Siri, switching</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> Wireless charging case adds a lot to the price</p><p>Apple's regular <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fshop%2Fselect-airpods\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">AirPods</a> package all the core features &#8212; like quick pairing with iOS devices and automatic playing and pausing &#8212; in a more affordable pair of wireless headphones. They're the right choice if convenience is your top priority in a pair of wireless earbuds, and if you'd rather sacrifice features like noise cancellation to save a few bucks.</p><p>Apple updated its standard AirPods in 2019, adding new features like the ability to use Siri hands-free and faster switching between devices. You also have the option to purchase AirPods with a wireless charging case, but that brings the price up to $199.&#160;</p><p>Unless you really hate plugging your <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fshop%2Fselect-airpods\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">AirPods</a> in with a Lightning cable and already own a wireless charger, we'd recommend either saving money by opting for the standard $159 pair or extending your budget to get the $249 <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FApple-AirPods-Pro%2F520468661\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">AirPods Pro</a>.</p><p>The AirPods that Apple launched in 2019 have the same design as the original model. That's to say they have a simple, white aesthetic with stems protruding from the bottom that essentially makes them look like Apple just snipped the wires off its wired EarPods headphones.&#160;</p><p>The standard AirPods are slightly lighter than the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FApple-AirPods-Pro%2F520468661\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">AirPods Pro</a> (4 grams versus 5.6 grams), and unlike the AirPods Pro they rest on the ear rather than inside it. That means the regular AirPods might be a better choice for those who prefer a less obtrusive fit.&#160;</p><p>All told, the standard AirPods are the best choice if convenience and affordability take priority over sound quality and noise cancellation when it comes to shopping for wireless earbuds.&#160;</p><h3>Read our full <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/apple-airpods-2-review-specs-features-photos-2019-4\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Apple AirPods review</a></h3>\n\tThe best AirPods for audiophiles\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5ffb7c8ebde805001980c13a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"AirPods Max 3\" height=\"750\" width=\"1000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lisa Eadicicco/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>At $549, the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fshop%2Fbuy-airpods%2Fairpods-max%3Fafid%3Dp239%257C10078%26cid%3Daos-us-aff-ir\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">AirPods Max</a> are the definition of luxury audio, offering superb sound quality, a premium and comfortable build, and top-notch noise cancellation.</h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Fit and style:</strong> Over-ear headphones with adjustable ear cups</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Battery life:</strong> Up to 20 hours</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Water resistant:</strong> No</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Features:</strong> Active noise cancellation, adaptive EQ, transparency mode, digital crown for media controls, Hey Siri, automatic switching, quick pairing, auto play and pause</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/apple-airpods-max-review\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Check out our full review of the AirPods Max</a></li></ul></aside><p><strong>Pros</strong>: Top-notch audio quality noise cancellation, premium design, comfortable fit&#160;</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> Expensive, no charging case, included case doesn't protect entire headset, no input options or included cables for other audio connections</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fshop%2Fbuy-airpods%2Fairpods-max\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">AirPods Max</a> deliver first-rate audio performance and noise cancellation, all wrapped in an elegant design that outclasses rivals from Bose and Sony.&#160;</p><p>The biggest difference you'll notice between the AirPods Max and Apple's other AirPods is its over-ear design. That alone suggests these headphones are designed for people that care more about audio quality than the average person, and also want a pair of headphones that make a statement when worn in public.&#160;</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fshop%2Fbuy-airpods%2Fairpods-max\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">AirPods Max</a> come with an Apple-designed driver and 10 audio cores for delivering computational audio and adaptive EQ, which allows the headphones to adjust their sound based on the fit of the ear cups. Like the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FApple-AirPods-Pro%2F520468661\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">AirPods Pro</a>, the AirPods Max also support spatial audio and other features like quick-pairing.&#160;</p><p>During my testing, I found that the AirPods Max sound significantly crisper, bolder, and louder than the $379 <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FBose-Noise-Cancelling-Wireless-Bluetooth-Headphones-700-in-Black%2F932544113\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Bose Noise Cancelling 700</a> headphones. They also outperformed the $350 Sony WH-1000XM4, although Sony's headphones came impressively close.&#160;</p><p>The AirPods Max also deliver when it comes to noise cancellation. When I sat underneath an elevated subway that runs above a very busy street near my apartment, the AirPods Max were able to significantly dull the sound of the train screeching to a halt and nearby traffic.&#160;&#160;</p><p>The downside, however, is that the included case doesn't charge the AirPods Pro.&#160; Instead, it puts them in low power mode.</p><p>There's no doubt that the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apple.com%2Fshop%2Fbuy-airpods%2Fairpods-max\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">AirPods Max</a> are excellent, but their price probably makes them inaccessible to most people. If you're an Apple loyalist that cares about having top notch audio and prefers over-ear designs &#8212; and are willing to splurge for it&#160; &#8212; the AirPods Max are the AirPods to get.&#160;</p><p>But most people should check out the significantly cheaper Sony <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FSony-WH-1000XM3-Wireless-Noise-Canceling-Over-Ear-Headphones%2F316361701\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">WH-1000XM4</a> headphones instead.</p>\n\tWhen will Apple release new AirPods?\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5c9bb4ba2cc740114a74b858?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Apple Airpods\" height=\"1549\" width=\"2065\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Hollis Johnson/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>Apple's standard AirPods are now in their second generation, while the AirPods Pro and AirPods Max are in their first generation. The release cycle for AirPods isn't as easy to predict as the iPhone's, but here's what we know based on reliable reports.&#160;</p><ul><li><strong>AirPods:</strong> Apple's second-generation AirPods launched in March 2019, and the company is said to be preparing a new pair of its least expensive wireless earbuds for launch in 2021. The new earbuds will have a new design with a shorter stem, longer battery life, and replaceable ear tips, according to <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2020-10-26/apple-developing-smaller-airpods-pro-revamped-entry-level-model\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Bloomberg</a>. That report says Apple had discussed launching the new AirPods in the first half of 2021. But TF International Securities analyst Ming-Chi Kuo <a href=\"https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/15/airpods-3-mass-production-q3-2021/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">has reported</a> that they won't go into mass production until the third quarter of 2021.</li><li><strong>AirPods Pro</strong>: Apple launched the AirPods Pro in October 2019. The company is working on a new redesigned version with a shorter stem that more closely resembles other wireless earbuds from brands like Samsung, according to <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2020-10-26/apple-developing-smaller-airpods-pro-revamped-entry-level-model\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Bloomberg</a>. But it's unclear when this new model would launch.</li><li><strong>AirPods Max</strong>: Apple just released the AirPods Max in December, and we have not heard any details about when a successor could launch.</li></ul>\n</div><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/best-apple-airpods'>Business Insider</a></div><div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a href=\"https://sec.report/AdviserInfo/Firms/137927/Form-ADV-137927.pdf\">regulatory filing</a> in late March that five of its funds hold crypto assets under custody with Coinbase. The amount and duration of investment is currently unclear.</p><p>In a separate brochure, the firm said it could invest in crypto directly or indirectly through derivatives contracts.</p><p>Coinbase recently disclosed it <a href=\"https://www.sec.gov/Archives/edgar/data/0001679788/000162828021006601/exhibit991-8xk.htm\">holds $122 billion</a> worth of institutional investments, which make up about 54% of the crypto exchange&#39;s total assets. The company expects to see &#34;meaningful growth&#34; through the remainder of the year, after raking in revenues of about $1.8 billion in the first-quarter of 2021, owing to increased institutional interest in crypto.</p><p>The exchange will <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/coinbase-plans-direct-listing-2-weeks-crypto-exchange-go-public-2021-4\">go public via a direct listing</a> on the Nasdaq this Wednesday.</p><p>Loeb&#39;s Third Point, which specializes in shareholder activism, may have taken the plunge into cryptocurrencies before the billionaire said last month he was <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/billionaire-investor-dan-loeb-exploring-cryptocurrencies-traditional-finance-controversial-ideas-2021-3-1030139581\">exploring the space</a>. &#34;I&#39;ve been doing a deep-dive into crypto lately,&#34; he said in a tweet at the time. &#34;It is a real test of being intellectually open to new and controversial ideas.&#34;</p><p>The hedge fund did not specify which cryptocurrencies it holds, but crypto investor <a href=\"https://twitter.com/APompliano/status/1380621049356824577\">Anthony Pompliano tweeted</a> that it&#39;s holding bitcoin.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60743d0f3e3fe7001882a113?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Screenshot 2021 04 12 at 13.28.41\" height=\"578\" width=\"1062\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p (Photo by Riccardo Savi/Getty Images for Concordia Summit)\" height=\"3000\" width=\"6000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Uber CEO Dara Khosrowshahi.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Riccardo Savi/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul><li><strong>Uber jumped as much as 4% on Monday after it revealed record gross-billings last month.</strong></li><li><strong>Uber&#39;s March business surge was driven by record Uber Eats billings and the strongest ride-hailing bookings since March 2020.</strong></li><li><strong>&#34;As vaccination rates increase in the United States, we are observing that consumer demand for Mobility is recovering faster than driver availability,&#34; Uber said.</strong></li><li><strong><a href=\"https://newsletter.businessinsider.com/join/4np/10-things-opening-bell?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestts&#38;utm_medium=ingest\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Sign up here for our daily newsletter, 10 Things Before the Opening Bell</a>.</strong></li></ul><hr><p><a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/uber-stock\">Uber</a> surged as much as 4% on Monday after it revealed in a business update that it experienced record gross-billings in March.</p><p>The business surge was driven by record gross billings in its delivery business, which crossed a $52 billion annualized gross bookings run-rate last month, representing year-over-year growth of more than 150%.</p><p>Uber&#39;s ride-hailing business was also strong in March, hitting its best levels since March 2020, which was the start of COVID-19 pandemic lockdowns spreading across the country. Uber said its ride-hailing business crossed the $30 billion annualized gross bookings run-rate, with average daily gross bookings up 9% month-over-month.</p><p>Uber sees the strong demand continuing, as more and more Americans are vaccinated and the economy fully reopens. According to <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/graphics/covid-vaccine-tracker-global-distribution/\">Bloomberg&#39;s vaccine tracker,</a> nearly a third of the US population has already received at least one COVID-19 vaccination dose. </p><p>&#34;As vaccination rates increase in the United States, we are observing that consumer demand for Mobility is recovering faster than driver availability, and consumer demand for Delivery continues to exceed courier availability,&#34; Uber said in <a href=\"https://d18rn0p25nwr6d.cloudfront.net/CIK-0001543151/84bcb1ae-108c-493b-a622-c8fcd2bb29b7.pdf\">a 8-K filed with the SEC. </a></p><p>To shore up the shortage in drivers, Uber said last week <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/uber-spending-250-million-driver-pay-pandemic-shortage-2021-4\">it is offering $250 million in temporary driver incentives</a> to get more Uber drivers back on the road.</p><p>With a business set to soar as the economy reopens, Uber continues to expect to reach quarterly adjusted EBITDA profitability in 2021, according to the SEC filing. </p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a Bell</a></li>\n</ul><p>Coinbase&#39;s debut on the Nasdaq on April 14 has been eagerly awaited, especially by cryptocurrency bulls who view the listing as a milestone for the digital currency ecosystem. <br><br>Adding to the excitement, the cryptocurrency trading giant reported a whopping <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/coinbase-earned-more-revenue-in-q1-than-all-of-2020-2021-4\">$1.8 billion revenue in the first quarter of the year</a> on Tuesday, compared to the $1.3 billion for all of 2020. </p><p>On the back of the eye-popping earnings, DA Davidson analyst Gil Luria <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/coinbase-price-target-raised-440-da-davidson-blockbuster-earnings-bitcoin-2021-4-1030282489\">increased his price target</a> by 125% to $440 from $195. The analyst derived his adjusted price target from a 20x multiple based on the company&#39;s expected revenue this year. <br><br>The record-breaking quarter for Coinbase moved in lockstep with bitcoin&#39;s surge, which thus far has soared more than 100% year-to-date and 600% in the past 12 months.  </p><p>The world&#39;s most popular cryptocurrency <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/bitcoin-price-btc-near-record-high-coinbase-ipo-cryptocurrencies-2021-4-1030293956?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestgest\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">rose as much as 2.6% to $61,229</a> on Monday as crypto advocates gear up for <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/coinbase-ipo-predictions-expert-analysis-direct-listing-bitcoin-crypto-2021-4-1030290743?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestgest\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Coinbase&#39;s direct listing. </a>The surge took the coin close to its all-time high of $61,742 reached on March 13.<br><br>Coinbase, the largest cryptocurrency exchange in the US, offers a wide range of products and services from trading and custody services to offering a stablecoin pegged to the US dollar. It has 43 million users in more than 100 countries. </p><p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/crypto-arbitrage-trading-strategy-alameda-research-sam-bankman-fried-billionaire-2021-4\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">A 29-year-old self-made billionaire breaks down how he achieved daily returns of 10% on million-dollar crypto trades, and shares how to find the best opportunities</a></em></p><p>Here&#39;s what eight crypto-industry experts had to say about Coinbase&#39;s public debut:</p><p dir=\"ltr\">&#34;The direct listing of Coinbase is a huge market signal, however, we&#39;re yet to see whether the long-term effect on the crypto industry will be positive or negative ... We are big fans of what Coinbase has done to date, but we worry about the centralizing effects of the concentration of users on a single platform, negating the true benefits of decentralization.&#34; - <strong>Alberto Jauregui, growth lead of <a href=\"https://pokt.network/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-saferedirecturl=\"https://www.google.com/url?q=https://pokt.network/&source=gmail&ust=1618071785530000&usg=AFQjCNFCFzOJrNiuuCyOflXUvhRn-dzNWQXUvhRn-dzNWQ\">Pocket Network</a>, a blockchain data ecosystem</strong></p><p dir=\"ltr\">&#34;The Coinbase listing is a huge step for the digital asset industry from both a mainstream adoption and regulatory point of view, signifying the acceptance of cryptocurrency business in traditional finance. Other exchanges following in Coinbase&#39;s footsteps are entirely based on their readiness to go public. This will pave the way for Coinbase&#39;s competitors to join the IPO movement. Kraken will most likely be next.&#34; - <strong>Gunnar Jaerv, COO of <a href=\"https://1stdigital.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-saferedirecturl=\"https://www.google.com/url?q=https://1stdigital.com/&source=gmail&ust=1618071785530000&usg=AFQjCNGEiuQsx1b-I4XQrotgyI1bX8tumgtgyI1bX8tumg\">First Digital Trust</a>, a leading digital asset custodian in Hong Kong</strong></p><p dir=\"ltr\">&#34;The success of Coinbase and its direct listing will bring on the next wave of new users to cryptocurrencies by continuing to solve the challenges of owning, storing, and providing custody to digital assets. This public listing will also have an enormous impact on the entire digital asset industry by opening the gate to further Wall Street and institutional investment and confirming that the future of finance is decentralized.&#34; - <strong>Leo Cheng, co-founder and project lead at <a href=\"https://app.cream.finance/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-saferedirecturl=\"https://www.google.com/url?q=https://app.cream.finance/&source=gmail&ust=1618071785530000&usg=AFQjCNEZ5WPEy08ooSPfb1W-T3sEuE9aMAW-T3sEuE9aMA\">C.R.E.A.M</a>. Finance, a decentralized lending protocol</strong></p><p dir=\"ltr\">&#34;Going public is stepping into the big leagues. Crypto is becoming part of the traditional finance sector ... This level of adoption seemed like a dream scenario just a year ago. A lot of users still keep funds on Coinbase and look at it as merely a trading platform. But more are beginning to wake up and understand that Coinbase is an important gateway to getting started in the crypto sector.&#34; - <strong>Kadan Stadelmann, CTO of <a href=\"https://komodoplatform.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-saferedirecturl=\"https://www.google.com/url?q=https://komodoplatform.com/&source=gmail&ust=1618071785530000&usg=AFQjCNGUbSoGFxI8sx1Fr3yKlP84M-17BQyKlP84M-17BQ\">Komodo</a>, an open-source technology workshop and blockchain solutions provider</strong></p><p dir=\"ltr\">&#34;When we entered into the market three years ago it was a new and novel industry, everyone had to wrap their heads around what we were doing as a business, the terminology we were using, and the potential value a bitcoin mining operation could hold. People saw us as a speculative gamble. This year we are seeing people move beyond that. Crypto is not a novel thing anymore, but the hot new asset class for equities.&#34; - <strong>Emiliano Grodzki, CEO of <a href=\"https://bitfarms.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-saferedirecturl=\"https://www.google.com/url?q=https://bitfarms.com/&source=gmail&ust=1618071785530000&usg=AFQjCNGvOqzoULKLItg-djMuIR1Id6SmPwMuIR1Id6SmPw\">Bitfarms</a>, a global public bitcoin mining operation</strong></p><p dir=\"ltr\">&#34;The growth and expansion of cryptocurrencies had always been at odds with the interests of traditional financial systems ... The Coinbase direct listing unites these two sides of finance in the success of this licensed and regulated company. Traditional investors who purchase Coinbase stock will indirectly speculate on the crypto market and similarly, crypto traders who own Coinbase stocks will have a vested interest in the success of the company.&#34; - <strong>James Anderson, CEO of <a href=\"https://riodefi.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-saferedirecturl=\"https://www.google.com/url?q=https://riodefi.com/&source=gmail&ust=1618071785530000&usg=AFQjCNHcXsnnzlkvPLJNi1innL69bVe06ginnL69bVe06g\">RioDeFi</a>, an ecosystem of interoperable financial products</strong></p><p dir=\"ltr\"> &#34;The Coinbase direct listing is going to further build credibility and legitimacy for the cryptocurrency markets, which have already received huge institutional interest and flows since the start of 2021. But once the celebrations settle and the mainstream awareness of the cryptocurrency markets grow, eyes will turn to the alternative burgeoning decentralized financial (DeFi) industry and structures like DAOs (decentralized autonomous organizations) will become common knowledge.&#34; - <strong>Samantha Yap Founder and CEO at <a href=\"https://yapglobal.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-saferedirecturl=\"https://www.google.com/url?q=https://yapglobal.com/&source=gmail&ust=1618071785531000&usg=AFQjCNEXd-0XJyhojHU4jVJjppjeNjdP0wJjppjeNjdP0w\">YAP Global</a>, a PR agency specializing in crypto, blockchain, and fintech</strong></p><p dir=\"ltr\">&#34;The Coinbase direct listing is going to be a bullish event for a host of reasons ... In the short term I expect to see a narrative forming that highlights the importance of A-tier [cryptocurrency exchanges] in the crypto ecosystem, but the narrative will then likely shift to focus on 00:43:06","updatedTime":"2021-04-13 00:43:06","title":"55 progressive groups urge Biden to go big on 'family-friendly care infrastructure'","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/progressive-groups-urge-biden-to-go-big-on-care-infrastructure-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606ddc6770954f0019195a80?format=jpeg\" alt=\"biden pittsburg infrastructure plan getty\" height=\"1663\" width=\"2217\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>President Joe Biden unveils part of his infrastructure plan in Pittsburgh on March 31.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Jim Watson/AFP/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>55 progressive groups called for Biden to invest in care infrastructure to support women and people of color.</li>\n<li>They called for a national paid and medical leave and permanent expansion of the Child Tax Credit.</li>\n<li>Democratic lawmakers have been advocating for those measures to be included in infrastructure.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The first $2.3 trillion part of the infrastructure package President Joe Biden <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-2-trillion-infrastructure-plan-roads-bridges-broadband-power-2021-3\">unveiled</a> on March 31 included some elements related to care-economy measures, like investments in home care. But progressive and liberal groups want Biden to go bigger on such measures in the next part of his plan.</p><p>Led by Invest in America and Care Can&#39;t Wait, 55 progressive groups called for Congress and the Biden administration to invest in care infrastructure to bring economic gains for women and communities of color, according to the <a href=\"https://investinamericanow.com/its-time-for-big-public-investment-in-a-care-infrastructure-that-works-for-everyone/\">letter</a>, which was first obtained by The Hill. The letter notes that over 2.3 million women left the labor force in 2020, of which more than 600,000 were Black women, and one in six child-care jobs lost during the pandemic have not returned.</p><p>&#34;It&#39;s time for the Biden administration and Congress to deliver for women by investing in a family-friendly care infrastructure that works for the millions of people who need care and support, those who have had to leave the workforce to become unpaid caregivers, and for the paid caregivers who have been historically undervalued,&#34; the letter said.</p><p>The letter, which was signed by the Service Employees International Union and MomsRising, said that to rebuild the economy, Biden must invest in measures including:</p><ul><li>High-quality child care and and long-term support services for aging adults and people with disabilities;</li><li>Creating millions of new care jobs and ensuring workers are paid family-sustaining wages with benefits and the option to unionize;</li><li>Creating a national paid family and medical leave program;</li><li>And updating the tax code to focus on women and communities of color, including permanently expanding the Child Tax Credit (CTC) and Earned Income Tax Credit (EITC).</li></ul><p>The letter also called for a pathway to citizenship for undocumented workers to provide them with economic security and opportunity.</p><p>Some of the measures the letter called for were already included in the first part of the infrastructure plan. For example, the plan proposed a <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-is-in-bidens-infrastructure-bill-package-american-jobs-plan-2021-3\">$400 billion investment</a> toward home and community care for the elderly and disabled, along with $48 billion toward an expansion of apprenticeships with a particular focus on women and people of color.</p><p>The letter echoes other efforts to encourage the creation of a national paid leave and a permanent expansion of tax credits. On April 5, House Ways and Means Committee Chair Richard Neal <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/child-care-infrastructure-plan-richard-neal-democrat-2021-4\">sent a letter</a> to Democratic committee members calling for the permanent expansion of the CTC and EITC, and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/democratic-senators-permanent-child-tax-credit-expanded-stimulus-2021-3\">41 Democratic senators</a> sent a letter to Biden on March 26 requesting the same thing.</p><p>Neal also said he will give every worker the right to paid family and medical leave in the infrastructure bill, and if employers or states already have paid leave policies in place, the bill will provide support to maintain and improve them.</p><p>Republican leadership argues that care-economy funding doesn&#39;t belong in an infrastructure bill. In a <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/mitch-mcconnell-slams-bidens-2-trillion-infrastructure-plan-missed-opportunity-2021-4\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"60\" data-uri=\"c95d458680660ca870686d7e463174d9\">statement two weeks ago</a>, Senate Minority Leader Mitch McConnell said that while Biden could have drafted a &#34;serious, targeted infrastructure plan&#34; that would have received bipartisan support, &#34;the latest liberal wish-list the White House has decided to label &#39;infrastructure&#39; is a major missed opportunity by this Administration.&#34;</p><p>The Biden administration is arguing for an <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/cecilia-rouse-america-needs-new-infrastructure-definition-2021-4\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"57cd0c1628845bd8e2c4d79ff9d62a55\">upgraded definition</a> of infrastructure. For instance, Cecilia Rouse, the chair of Biden&#39;s Council of Economic Advisors, said in an April 3 CBS News interview that the care economy is a major part of the 21st century economy and therefore deserves inclusion.</p><p>Biden is expected to unveil the second part of his infrastructure plan in mid-April.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/progressive-groups-urge-biden-to-go-big-on-care-infrastructure-2021-4'>Business Insider</a></div><div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a and is likely to see a boom in growth and hiring, but still faces threats from COVID-19.</p><p>&#34;The outlook has brightened substantially,&#34; he told CBS&#39;s &#34;60 minutes.&#34; Yet he said there was a risk that coronavirus starts spreading again.</p><p><a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/jerome-powell-federal-reserve-digital-dollar-china-yuan-cbdc-2021-4-1030293157\">He also discussed the outlook for a digital dollar</a>, and said the the US central bank is working hard on researching one as nervousness grows in some quarters about China&#39;s rapid development of its own digital currency.</p><p>As the economy continues to recover from the pandemic, investors are focused in on inflation data that is due Tuesday. 00:43:06","updatedTime":"2021-04-13 00:43:06","title":"A majority of CEOs say Biden's proposed corporate tax hike could undo the economic gains from Trump's cuts","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-tax-plan-corporate-rate-increase-jobs-wage-growth-survey-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/602fe7b88b93230018712748?format=jpeg\" alt=\"uncle sam taxes\" height=\"768\" width=\"1024\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Uncle Sam. Ben Sklar / Stringer/Getty Images\n<p class=\"copyright\">Ben Sklar / Stringer/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>A majority of US CEOs are saying Biden&#39;s corporate tax increase would negatively affect business.</li>\n<li>Wage growth, hiring, and research and development spending would slow as a result, the CEOs said. </li>\n<li>Biden proposed upping the corporate tax rate to 28% from 21%, but has since said he may compromise.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>American business leaders are warning a corporate tax rate hike <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-2-trillion-infrastructure-plan-roads-bridges-broadband-power-2021-3\">proposed</a> by President Joe Biden could make it harder to hire workers and increase their wages.</p><p>In a survey of 178 CEOs conducted by the Business Round Table published Monday, a majority of respondents said the increase - from 21% to 28% - put forward by the White House in March would hinder economic expansion, research and development spending, wage growth, and hiring.</p><p>The results showed:</p><ul><li>98% of CEOs said the increase would have a &#34;moderate&#34; to &#34;very&#34; significant adverse impact on competitiveness;</li><li>75% said it would negatively affect spending on research and development; </li><li>71% said it would negatively affect their ability to hire; and</li><li>about 66% said it would slow US wage growth.</li></ul><p>&#34;As we look toward recovering from the COVID-19 pandemic, keeping competitive tax policies in place is needed to help reinvigorate the U.S. economy and lead to more opportunity for Americans,&#34; Gregory J. Hayes, chief executive of Raytheon and chair of the Business Roundtable Tax and Fiscal Policy Committee, said in a release.</p><p><em><strong>Read more: </strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/post-covid-pandemic-productivity-boom-will-reshape-work-boost-economy-2021-4\">The post-COVID productivity boom is going to let us dump the unproductive parts of virtual working and keep the good parts</a></em></p><p>Biden&#39;s revealed his <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-2-trillion-infrastructure-plan-roads-bridges-broadband-power-2021-3\">$2 trillion infrastructure plan</a> last month, which included spending on upgrading roads, bridges, and affordable housing, paid for in part by the corporate tax increase. The president has since said he may agree to <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-2-trillion-infrastructure-plan-roads-bridges-broadband-power-2021-3\">compromise with a 25% rate</a>, instead of the originally proposed 28%. </p><p>Amazon CEO Jeff Bezos has been on of the few to say his firm<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-supports-corporate-tax-hike-biden-infrastructure-plan-bezos-says-2021-4\"> supports the tax increase,</a> calling the move &#34;a bold investment in American infrastructure.&#34;</p><p>But in the Business Round Table survey, Hayes said the lower corporate tax rate from before the pandemic &#34;drove economic growth, creating 6 million jobs, pushing the unemployment rate to a 50-year low and increasing middle class wages.&#34;</p><p>In 2017 under the Trump administration, the government lowered the corporate tax rate to 21% with the Tax Cuts and Jobs Act. But it may not have turned out to be the <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/7-charts-showing-trump-tax-cuts-not-economic-rocket-fuel-2019-12-1028780773\">economic &#34;rocket fuel&#34;</a> he had promised. </p><p>The Tax Policy Center, an independent research group created by the Urban Institute and Brookings Institution, actually found &#34;<a href=\"https://www.taxpolicycenter.org/taxvox/new-congressional-study-finds-little-economic-benefit-2017-tax-cuts\">little economic benefit</a>&#34; from the 2017 law, saying it largely benefited corporations and created only modest wage growth. </p><p>Biden decried the former president&#39;s tax cuts, saying he&#39;s &#34;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-corporate-tax-hike-infrastructure-big-companies-average-americans-2021-4\">sick and tired</a> of ordinary people being fleeced.&#34; </p><p>But according to the Tax Foundation, an independent tax policy nonprofit, Biden&#39;s tax plan would <a href=\"https://files.taxfoundation.org/20200928134201/Details-and-Analysis-of-Democratic-Presidential-Nominee-Joe-Bidens-Tax-Proposals-September-2020-Update.pdf\">cut economic output by 1.47%</a> over the long-term, causing a 1% lower wage rate and 518,000 fewer full-time jobs.</p><p>&#34;The proposed tax increases on job creators would slow America&#39;s recovery and hurt workers,&#34; Joshua Bolten, president and CEO of the Business Roundtable, said. </p><p>The heavily pro-corporate interest Business Roundtable was formed in 1972 and represents nearly every sector of the American economy. Its membership rolls currently include 3M, American Airlines, Amazon, and Coca-Cola, and more. </p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-tax-plan-corporate-rate-increase-jobs-wage-growth-survey-2021-4'>Business Insider</a></div><div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a vehicle manufacturer to Buy in a Monday note.</p><p>Canaccord assigned a $1,071 price target to Tesla, representing potential upside of 58% from Friday&#39;s close, according to the note.</p><p>&#34;Tesla&#39;s focus on first-principle engineering we believe will radically change the battery market, enabling the company to further the lead in [battery electric vehicles] and Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/riot-stock\"></a></p><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Riot Blockchain stock jumped as much as 12% on Monday amid Bitcoin&#39;s brief run above $60,000.</li>\n<li>The cryptocurrency mining company also announced an 80% increase in mining production.</li>\n<li>Riot produced 187 bitcoin in March alone and 491 bitcoin in the first quarter of 2021. </li>\n<li aria-level=\"1\"><strong><a href=\"https://newsletter.businessinsider.com/join/4np/10-things-opening-bell?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestm=ingest\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Sign up here for our daily newsletter, 10 Things Before the Opening Bell.</a></strong></li>\n</ul><p><a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/riot-stock\">Riot Blockchain&#39;s</a> stock jumped as much as 12% on Monday after the company announced an 80% increase in bitcoin mining production and the cryptocurrency briefly pushed <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/bitcoin-price-btc-near-record-high-coinbase-ipo-cryptocurrencies-2021-4-1030293956\">past $60,000 per coin</a>.</p><p>In a <a href=\"https://www.riotblockchain.com/news-media/press-releases/detail/105/riot-blockchain-announces-march-production-and-operations\">press release</a> that came out early Monday morning, Riot Blockchain said that in March 2021, it produced 187 bitcoin. That&#39;s 80% more than the company&#39;s mining operations produced a year ago, before bitcoin&#39;s halving.</p><p>A <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/bitcoin-undergoes-third-halving-falls-vs-us-dollar-2020-5\">bitcoin &#34;halving&#34;</a> is when the reward for mining Bitcoin transactions is cut in half. The last halving occurred on May 11, 2020.</p><p>The 80% jump in bitcoin mining production despite a tough comparison from the pre-halving quarter is illustrative of Riot&#39;s continued push for mining dominance.</p><p>Riot produced 491 bitcoin in the first quarter of 2021, an increase of 75% over its pre-halving first quarter 2020 production of 281 BTC.</p><p>The bitcoin mining company now holds some 1,565 bitcoin on its balance sheet, worth roughly $94 million at current prices, according to <a href=\"https://www.riotblockchain.com/news-media/press-releases/detail/103/riot-blockchain-announces-milestone-purchase-order-of\">data from the company</a>.</p><p>The news of Riot&#39;s rising bitcoin production comes after the firm <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/riot-blockchain-acquire-largest-north-american-bitcoin-hosting-facility-whinestone-2021-4-1030286353\">inked a deal to acquire</a> the largest bitcoin mining facility in North America, Whinstone US, for roughly $650 million last week.</p><p>Riot also recently <a href=\"https://www.riotblockchain.com/news-media/press-releases/detail/103/riot-blockchain-announces-milestone-purchase-order-of\">announced</a> that it picked up an additional 42,000 S19j Antminers from Bitmain for $138.5 million on April 7.</p><p>By the fourth quarter of 2022, the firm expects to have a total hash rate capacity of 7.7 exahash per second (EH/s) and a fleet of roughly 81,146 Antminers.</p><p>Riot also recently bolstered its management team with the addition of Megan Brooks as Chief Operating Officer, Phil McPherson as Vice President of Capital Markets, and Ryan Werner as Vice President of Finance.</p><p>HC Wainwright &#38; Co. reiterated its &#34;buy&#34; rating on shares of Riot and tagged the firm with a $64 price target on April 1 as well.</p><p>Shares of Riot traded up 8.75% as of 11:28 a.m. ET on Monday.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/607467473e3fe7001882a1b6?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Riot chart 4\" height=\"670\" width=\"820\" class=\"copyright\">Zakiyyah Woods for Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\t\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/607337f6a451820019b3a763?format=jpeg\" alt=\"LunaParkReopen_08.JPG\" height=\"864\" width=\"860\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A young girl waits for a ride to begin.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Zakiyyah Woods for Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\t\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/607335e2a451820019b3a75e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"LunaParkReopens_01.JPG\" height=\"650\" width=\"864\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Members of the Brooklyn United drum-line pictured in front of the iconic Cyclone roller coaster.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Zakiyyah Woods for Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\t\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6072e551a451820019b3a72a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"LunaParkReopen_02.JPG\" height=\"836\" width=\"864\" Woods</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\t\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60733fbf4943790018bb1d3c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"LunaParkReopen_17.JPG\" height=\"496\" width=\"864\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>An employee of Deno’s Wonder Wheel Amusement Park sanitizes a ride in between visitors.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Zakiyyah Woods for Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n</div><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a
